<script type="rocketlazyloadscript">document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', function() {
    const ratingContainers = document.querySelectorAll('.tasty-rating-display');

    ratingContainers.forEach(container => {
        const stars = container.querySelectorAll('.star-link');
        let selectedRating = 0;

        stars.forEach(star => {
            const starValue = parseInt(star.dataset.star);

            // Hover: highlight all stars up to hovered star
            star.addEventListener('mouseenter', () => {
                stars.forEach(s => {
                    const sValue = parseInt(s.dataset.star);
                    if (sValue <= starValue) {
                        s.querySelector('.star').classList.add('hovered');
                    } else {
                        s.querySelector('.star').classList.remove('hovered');
                    }
                });
            });

            // Remove hover on mouse leave of container
            container.addEventListener('mouseleave', () => {
                stars.forEach(s => s.querySelector('.star').classList.remove('hovered'));
                // Restore selection
                stars.forEach(s => {
                    const sValue = parseInt(s.dataset.star);
                    if (sValue <= selectedRating) {
                        s.querySelector('.star').classList.add('selected');
                    } else {
                        s.querySelector('.star').classList.remove('selected');
                    }
                });
            });

            // Click: set selection & keep it
            star.addEventListener('click', e => {
                e.preventDefault();
                selectedRating = starValue;
                container.dataset.selectedRating = selectedRating;

                stars.forEach(s => {
                    const sValue = parseInt(s.dataset.star);
                    if (sValue <= selectedRating) {
                        s.querySelector('.star').classList.add('selected');
                    } else {
                        s.querySelector('.star').classList.remove('selected');
                    }
                });

                // Scroll or jump to #respond if needed
                const respond = document.querySelector('#respond');
                if (respond) {
                    respond.scrollIntoView({behavior: 'smooth'});
                    respond.querySelector('textarea, input[type="text"]').focus();
                }
            });

            // Keyboard accessibility: Enter or Space to select
            star.addEventListener('keydown', e => {
                if (e.key === 'Enter' || e.key === ' ') {
                    e.preventDefault();
                    star.click();
                }
            });
        });

        // Initialize: if rating exists, mark selected stars
        const initialRating = parseInt(container.dataset.selectedRating) || 0;
        if (initialRating > 0) {
            stars.forEach(s => {
                const sValue = parseInt(s.dataset.star);
                if (sValue <= initialRating) {
                    s.querySelector('.star').classList.add('selected');
                }
            });
        }
    });
});
